NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
VICTORY EDUCATIONAL TRUST
No. 5, Anna Garden, Velachery Main Road, Velachery, Chennai-600 042.
This is to inform the general public that M/s. “Victory Educational Trust” established on 24th September 2007 our
Founder-cum-President Mr. C. Frederic Kenneth, son of G.M. Cecil, residing at No. 33, Chetty Street, Saidapet, Chennai600 015 (based on our records) Resigned his post on 13th January 2010 his resignation accepted by trust board and it has
been effected from 14th January 2010. Based on his resignation trust board appointed new trustees Founder Mr. Arun
Jeyapaul and President Mr. R. Vijay Anand with effect from 14th January 2010. From the date of his resignation trust board
will not bind any correspondence made by him on behalf of our trust.
Chennai,
26th May 2010.

For VICTORY EDUCATIONAL TRUST,
R. VIJAY ANAND.
ARUN JEYAPAUL.
Trustees.
